[30;1m105 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m106 | [0m[35m* Breaking change: the dependency on ``httplib2`` has been replaced by[0m
[30;1m107 | [0m[35m  an internal ``couchdb.http`` library. This changes the API in several places.[0m

[30;1m110 | [0m[35m  This better reflects what is actually provided. Classes inside[0m
[30;1m111 | [0m[35m  ``couchdb.mapping`` have been similarly renamed (e.g. ``Schema`` -> ``Mapping``).[0m
